```markdown
// app/api/users/route.ts
import { NextResponse } from 'next/server'
import { auth } from '@/lib/auth'

export async function GET(request: Request) {
  const session = await auth()

  if (!session) {
    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: 'Unauthorized' },
      { status: 401 }
    )
  }

  // å®ç°é€»è¾‘
  const users = await db.user.findMany()

  return NextResponse.json(users)
}
```

```json
    "restrict_by_path": {
      "src/": {
        "allow": ["ReadFile", "WriteFile"]
      },
      "scripts/": {
        "deny": ["ExecuteBash"]
      },
      "config/": {
        "ask": ["WriteFile"]
      }
    }
  }
}
```

##### è‡ªå®šä¹‰ MCP æœåŠ¡å™¨

**åˆ›å»ºç®€å•çš„ MCP Server**

**1. åˆå§‹åŒ–é¡¹ç›®**

```bash
# åˆ›å»ºç›®å½•
mkdir my-mcp-server
cd my-mcp-server

# åˆå§‹åŒ–
npm init -y

# å®‰è£…ä¾èµ–
npm install @modelcontextprotocol/sdk
```

**2. å®ç° Server**

**src/index.ts**

```typescript
import { Server } from "@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/index.js";
import { StdioServerTransport } from "@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/server/stdio.js";

const server = new Server(
  {
    name: "my-custom-server",
    version: "1.0.0",
  },
  {
    capabilities: {
      tools: {},
    },
  }
);

// å®šä¹‰å·¥å…·
server.setRequestHandler("tools/list", async () => {
  return {
    tools: [
      {
        name: "greet",
        description: "Greet a user",
        inputSchema: {
          type: "object",
          properties: {
            name: {
              type: "string",
              description: "Name to greet",
            },
          },
          required: ["name"],
        },
      },
    ],
  };
});

// å®ç°å·¥å…·
server.setRequestHandler("tools/call", async (request) => {
  if (request.params.name === "greet") {
    const name = request.params.arguments?.name;
    return {
      content: [
        {
          type: "text",
          text: `Hello, ${name}!`,
        },
      ],
    };
  }

  throw new Error(`Unknown tool: ${request.params.name}`);
});

// å¯åŠ¨ server
const transport = new StdioServerTransport();
await server.connect(transport);
```

**3. é…ç½® package.json**

```json
{
  "name": "my-mcp-server",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "type": "module",
  "bin": {
    "my-mcp-server": "./dist/index.js"
  },
  "scripts": {
    "build": "tsc",
    "start": "node dist/index.js"
  }
}
```

**4. ç¼–è¯‘å’Œæµ‹è¯•**

```bash
# ç¼–è¯‘
npm run build

# æµ‹è¯•
node dist/index.js
```

**5. é…ç½®åˆ° Claude Code**

**~/.claude/mcp.json**

```json
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "my-custom-server": {
      "command": "node",
      "args": ["/path/to/my-mcp-server/dist/index.js"]
    }
  }
}
```

**6. ä½¿ç”¨è‡ªå®šä¹‰ Server**

```bash
# å¯åŠ¨ Claude Code
claude

# æµ‹è¯•å·¥å…·
ä½¿ç”¨ my-custom-server æ‰“æ‹›å‘¼ç»™ Alice
```

---

##### MCP é…ç½®æ¨¡æ¿

**å®Œæ•´é…ç½®ç¤ºä¾‹**

**~/.claude/mcp.json**

```json
{
  "mcpServers": {
    "github": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": [
        "-y",
        "@modelcontextprotocol/server-github"
      ],
      "env": {
        "GITHUB_PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN": "${GITHUB_TOKEN}"
      }
    },
    "postgres": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": [
        "-y",
        "@modelcontextprotocol/server-postgres",
        "${POSTGRES_CONNECTION_STRING}"
      ]
    },
    "supabase": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": [
        "-y",
        "@modelcontextprotocol/server-supabase"
      ],
      "env": {
        "SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN": "${SUPABASE_TOKEN}"
      }
    },
    "sentry": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": [
        "-y",
        "@modelcontextprotocol/server-sentry"
      ],
      "env": {
        "SENTRY_AUTH_TOKEN": "${SENTRY_TOKEN}",
        "SENTRY_ORG_SLUG": "my-org"
      }
    },
    "slack": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": [
        "-y",
        "@modelcontextprotocol/server-slack"
      ],
      "env": {
        "SLACK_BOT_TOKEN": "${SLACK_BOT_TOKEN}",
        "SLACK_TEAM_ID": "${SLACK_TEAM_ID}"
      }
    },
    "playwright": {
      "command": "npx",
      "args": [
        "-y",
        "@modelcontextprotocol/server-playwright"
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

```yaml
# æµ‹è¯•ç¼–å†™æŒ‡å—

## æµ‹è¯•åŸåˆ™

1. **AAA æ¨¡å¼**
   - Arrangeï¼ˆå‡†å¤‡ï¼‰
   - Actï¼ˆæ‰§è¡Œï¼‰
   - Assertï¼ˆæ–­è¨€ï¼‰

2. **æµ‹è¯•è¦†ç›–**

   - é”™è¯¯åœºæ™¯

   - æ ¼å¼ï¼š`should_ExpectedBehavior_When_Condition`

## æµ‹è¯•æ¨¡æ¿

\`\`\`typescript
describe('UserService', () => {
  describe('createUser', () => {
    it('should create user with valid data', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const userData = {
        name: 'John Doe',
        email: 'john@example.com'
      }

      // Act
      const user = await userService.createUser(userData)

      // Assert
      expect(user.id).toBeDefined()
      expect(user.name).toBe(userData.name)
      expect(user.email).toBe(userData.email)
    })

    it('should throw error when email is invalid', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const userData = {
        name: 'John Doe',
        email: 'invalid-email'
      }

      // Act & Assert
      await expect(
        userService.createUser(userData)
      ).rejects.toThrow('Invalid email format')
    })
  })
})
\`\`\`
```

```markdown
\`\`\`typescript
// âœ… å¥½çš„åšæ³•
async function fetchUser(id: string): Promise<User> {
  try {
    const response = await api.get(`/users/${id}`)
    return userSchema.parse(response.data)
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof ZodError) {
      throw new ValidationError('Invalid user data', error)
    }
    if (error instanceof ApiError && error.status === 404) {
      throw new NotFoundError(`User ${id} not found`)
    }
    throw new UnknownError('Failed to fetch user', error)
  }
}
\`\`\`

  id: string
  name: string
  email: string
  role: 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest'
}

  return user.role === 'admin'
}

// âŒ é¿å…

  return user.role === 'admin'
```

```markdown
describe('functionName', () => {
  it('should handle normal case', () => {
    const result = functionName(validInput)
    expect(result).toBe(expectedOutput)
  })

  it('should handle edge case', () => {
    const result = functionName(edgeInput)
    expect(result).toBe(expectedOutput)
  })

  it('should handle error case', () => {
    expect(() => functionName(invalidInput))
      .toThrow('Expected error')
  })
})
```

**æŸ¥çœ‹ Worktrees**

```bash
# è¾“å‡ºç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š
```

**åˆ é™¤ Worktree**

```bash
# æ–¹æ³• 1: ä½¿ç”¨ Git å‘½ä»¤ï¼ˆæ¨èï¼‰

# å¦‚æœæœ‰æœªæäº¤çš„æ›´æ”¹

# æ–¹æ³• 2: æ‰‹åŠ¨åˆ é™¤ + æ¸…ç†
```

**æŠ€å·§ 2: æ‰¹é‡æ“ä½œ**

```bash
# è·å–æ‰€æœ‰ worktrees

  echo "Updating: $path"
  cd "$path"
  git pull
  npm install  # æˆ–å…¶ä»–æ›´æ–°å‘½ä»¤
```

```bash
# 3. é“¾æ¥å›¢é˜Ÿèµ„æº

  echo "åˆ›å»º mcp.json..."

  echo "âš ï¸  è¯·é…ç½® MCP tokens åœ¨ ~/.claude/.env"

# GitHub

# Sentry

# Slack

EOF
  echo "âš ï¸  è¯·å¡«å†™ ~/.claude/.env ä¸­çš„ tokens"
fi

echo "âœ… å›¢é˜Ÿé…ç½®å®‰è£…å®Œæˆï¼"
echo ""
echo "ä¸‹ä¸€æ­¥ï¼š"
echo "1. å¡«å†™ ~/.claude/.env ä¸­çš„ API tokens"
echo "2. è¿è¡Œ 'claude' æµ‹è¯•é…ç½®"
```

# scripts/check-claude-md.sh

#!/bin/bash

# 1. æ£€æŸ¥æ–‡ä»¶å­˜åœ¨

  "é¡¹ç›®ç»“æ„"

  echo "âš ï¸  å»ºè®®æ·»åŠ ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹"

  echo "âš ï¸  CLAUDE.md å¤ªçŸ­ï¼Œå»ºè®®æ·»åŠ æ›´å¤šå†…å®¹"

````markdown
ä½ æ˜¯å›¢é˜Ÿçš„æµ‹è¯•ä¸“å®¶ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆç¬¦åˆå›¢é˜Ÿæ ‡å‡†çš„æµ‹è¯•ã€‚

## æµ‹è¯•æ¡†æ¶

- å•å…ƒæµ‹è¯•: Vitest
- E2E æµ‹è¯•: Playwright
- ç»„ä»¶æµ‹è¯•: Testing Library

## æµ‹è¯•æ¨¡æ¿

### React ç»„ä»¶æµ‹è¯•

```typescript
import { render, screen } from '@testing-library/react';
import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
import { ComponentName } from './component-name';

describe('ComponentName', () => {
  it('renders correctly', () => {
    render(<ComponentName />);
    expect(screen.getByText('Expected Text')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('handles user interaction', async () => {
    const { user } = render(<ComponentName />);
    await user.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(screen.getByText('Result')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});
```

### API æµ‹è¯•

```typescript
import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
import { api } from './api';

describe('API: /users', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    // Setup
  });

  it('GET /users returns user list', async () => {
    const response = await api.get('/users');
    expect(response.status).toBe(200);
    expect(response.data).toHaveLength(10);
  });

  it('POST /users creates new user', async () => {
    const newUser = { name: 'John' };
    const response = await api.post('/users', newUser);
    expect(response.status).toBe(201);
    expect(response.data.name).toBe('John');
  });
});
```
````

**Claude Code è‡ªåŠ¨å®¡æŸ¥**

**GitHub Action é›†æˆ**

**.github/workflows/claude-review.yml**

```yaml
name: Claude Code Review

on:
  pull_request:
    types: [opened, synchronize]

jobs:
  claude-review:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Setup Node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'

      - name: Install Claude Code
        run: npm install -g @anthropic/claude-code

      - name: Run Code Review
        env:
          ANTHROPIC_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY }}
        run: |
          claude -p "
          è¯·å®¡æŸ¥è¿™ä¸ª PR çš„æ‰€æœ‰æ›´æ”¹ã€‚

          é‡ç‚¹å…³æ³¨ï¼š
          1. ä»£ç è´¨é‡
          2. å®‰å…¨é—®é¢˜
          3. æ€§èƒ½é—®é¢˜
          4. æµ‹è¯•è¦†ç›–

          æä¾›è¯¦ç»†çš„å®¡æŸ¥æŠ¥å‘Šã€‚
          " > review.md

      - name: Post Review Comment
        uses: actions/github-script@v7
        with:
          script: |
            const fs = require('fs');
            const review = fs.readFileSync('review.md', 'utf8');

            github.rest.issues.createComment({
              issue_number: context.issue.number,
              owner: context.repo.owner,
              repo: context.repo.repo,
              body: `## ğŸ¤– Claude Code è‡ªåŠ¨å®¡æŸ¥\n\n${review}`
            });
```

```bash
# æ”¶é›†æŒ‡æ ‡
# scripts/team-metrics.sh

#!/bin/bash

echo "ğŸ“Š å›¢é˜Ÿ Claude Code ä½¿ç”¨ç»Ÿè®¡"
echo ""

# 1. PR åˆ›å»ºåˆ°åˆå¹¶æ—¶é—´
echo "PR å¹³å‡å¤„ç†æ—¶é—´:"
gh pr list --state merged --json createdAt,mergedAt --jq '
  map((.mergedAt | fromdateiso8601) - (.createdAt | fromdateiso8601)) |
  add / length / 3600 | floor
' | xargs echo "å°æ—¶"

# 2. ä»£ç å®¡æŸ¥æ—¶é—´
echo ""
echo "ä»£ç å®¡æŸ¥å¹³å‡æ—¶é—´:"
# ...

# 3. æ¯å‘¨ PR æ•°é‡
echo ""
echo "æœ¬å‘¨ PR æ•°é‡:"
gh pr list --state all --search "created:>=$(date -v-7d +%Y-%m-%d)" --json number | jq 'length'

# 4. Claude Code ä½¿ç”¨ç‡
echo ""
echo "Claude Code ä½¿ç”¨æƒ…å†µ:"
# ç»Ÿè®¡åŒ…å« "Generated with Claude Code" çš„ commits
git log --all --since="1 week ago" --grep="Claude Code" --oneline | wc -l | xargs echo "commits"
```

```bash
# scripts/cost-report.sh

#!/bin/bash

echo "ğŸ’° å›¢é˜Ÿ Claude Code æˆæœ¬æŠ¥å‘Š"
echo ""

TEAM_MEMBERS=("alice" "bob" "charlie")

TOTAL_COST=0

for member in "${TEAM_MEMBERS[@]}"; do
  COST=$(claude --user $member -p "/usage" | grep "æœ¬æœˆæˆæœ¬" | awk '{print $2}')
  echo "$member: \$$COST"
  TOTAL_COST=$(echo "$TOTAL_COST + $COST" | bc)
done

echo ""
echo "æ€»è®¡: \$$TOTAL_COST"
echo ""

# è®¡ç®— ROI
TEAM_SIZE=${#TEAM_MEMBERS[@]}
HOURS_SAVED=$(echo "$TEAM_SIZE * 10 * 4" | bc)  # æ¯äººæ¯å‘¨ 10 å°æ—¶
VALUE=$(echo "$HOURS_SAVED * 50" | bc)  # $50/å°æ—¶
ROI=$(echo "scale=2; $VALUE / $TOTAL_COST" | bc)

echo "æ—¶é—´èŠ‚çœ: $HOURS_SAVED å°æ—¶/æœˆ"
echo "ä»·å€¼: \$$VALUE"
echo "ROI: ${ROI}x"
```

#### æ€§èƒ½ç›‘æ§è„šæœ¬

**æˆæœ¬ç›‘æ§è„šæœ¬**

```bash
# ~/scripts/claude-cost-monitor.sh

#!/bin/bash

LOG_FILE=~/.claude/cost-log.txt
DATE=$(date +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M")

# è·å–å½“å‰æˆæœ¬
COST=$(claude --output-format json -p "/cost" | jq -r '.estimated_cost')

# è®°å½•
echo "$DATE,$COST" >> $LOG_FILE

# æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦è¶…è¿‡é˜ˆå€¼
THRESHOLD=10.0
if (( $(echo "$COST > $THRESHOLD" | bc -l) )); then
  echo "âš ï¸  è­¦å‘Š: æˆæœ¬ $COST è¶…è¿‡é˜ˆå€¼ $THRESHOLD"

  # å‘é€é€šçŸ¥ï¼ˆmacOSï¼‰
  osascript -e "display notification \"æˆæœ¬: \$$COST\" with title \"Claude Code æˆæœ¬è­¦å‘Š\""

  # æˆ–å‘é€é‚®ä»¶ã€Slack ç­‰
fi

# æ˜¾ç¤ºä»Šæ—¥ç»Ÿè®¡
TODAY=$(date +"%Y-%m-%d")
TODAY_COST=$(grep "$TODAY" $LOG_FILE | awk -F',' '{sum+=$2} END {printf "%.2f", sum}')
echo "ä»Šæ—¥æ€»æˆæœ¬: \$$TODAY_COST"
```

#### CI/CD é›†æˆ

**GitHub Actions é›†æˆ**

**1. è‡ªåŠ¨åŒ–æµ‹è¯•**

**.github/workflows/test.yml**

```yaml
name: Tests

on: [push, pull_request]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
      - run: npm ci
      - run: npm test
```

**2. Claude Code è‡ªåŠ¨å®¡æŸ¥**

**.github/workflows/claude-review.yml**

```yaml
name: Claude Code Review

on:
  pull_request:
    types: [opened, synchronize]

jobs:
  review:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Claude Code Review
        run: |
          claude -p "Review this PR and provide feedback" \
            --output-format json > review.json
      - name: Post Comment
        uses: actions/github-script@v7
        with:
          script: |
            const review = require('./review.json')
            github.rest.issues.createComment({
              issue_number: context.issue.number,
              owner: context.repo.owner,
              repo: context.repo.repo,
              body: review.content
            })
```

**æœ¬åœ° CI æµ‹è¯•**

```bash
# åœ¨æäº¤å‰è¿è¡Œå®Œæ•´ CI æµç¨‹
! npm run ci

# åŒ…å«ï¼š
# - Linting
# - Type checking
# - Unit tests
# - Integration tests
# - Build
```

### 4.2 å¿«é€Ÿå‚è€ƒè¡¨

> å¿«é€ŸæŸ¥è¯¢å¡ç‰‡ - é€‚åˆæ‰“å°ä½¿ç”¨

#### 4.2.1 å¿«æ·é”®é€ŸæŸ¥è¡¨

**ğŸ¹ äº¤äº’æ¨¡å¼å¿«æ·é”®**

| å¿«æ·é”® | åŠŸèƒ½ |
|-------|------|
| `Tab` | åˆ‡æ¢ Extended Thinkingï¼ˆæ·±åº¦æ€è€ƒæ¨¡å¼ï¼‰ |
| `Shift+Tab` | åˆ‡æ¢æƒé™æ¨¡å¼ï¼ˆDefault â†” Plan â†” Auto-Acceptï¼‰ |
| `Alt+M` | åˆ‡æ¢æƒé™æ¨¡å¼ï¼ˆåŒä¸Šï¼‰ |
| `Ctrl+C` | ä¸­æ–­å½“å‰æ“ä½œ |
| `Ctrl+L` | æ¸…é™¤å±å¹•ï¼ˆä¿ç•™å†å²ï¼‰ |
| `Ctrl+O` | åˆ‡æ¢è¯¦ç»†è¾“å‡º |
| `Ctrl+R` | æœç´¢å‘½ä»¤å†å² |
| `Esc` `Esc` | å›æ»šæœ€åæ“ä½œ |

**ğŸ’» IDE é›†æˆå¿«æ·é”®**

**VS Code**

| å¿«æ·é”® | åŠŸèƒ½ |
|-------|------|
| `Cmd+K` (Mac) / `Ctrl+K` (Win) | å¿«é€Ÿæ‰“å¼€ Claude Code |
| `@filename` | å¼•ç”¨æ–‡ä»¶ |
| `Tab` | åˆ‡æ¢ Extended Thinking |
| `Shift+Tab` | åˆ‡æ¢æƒé™æ¨¡å¼ |

**JetBrains IDE**

| å¿«æ·é”® (Mac) | å¿«æ·é”® (Win/Linux) | åŠŸèƒ½ |
|-------------|-------------------|------|
